SELECT [b].[BlogPostId], [b].[CategoryId], [c].[Id], [c].[Description], [c].[Name]
FROM [BlogPostCategory] AS [b]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT DISTINCT [bp].[ModifiedAt], [bp].[PublishOn], [bp].[Id]
    FROM (
        SELECT * from [dbo].[BlogPost] WHERE Contains((Content, Description, Title), @p0)
    ) AS [bp]
